	<string id=0 seek=1933368>Status Junction Explanation</string>
	<string id=1 seek=1933396>By junctioning a GF with

	<string id=2 seek=1933448>as magic is junctioned,</string>

	<string id=5 seek=1933564>see the Status Junction screen.</string>

	<string id=7 seek=1933656>First, select a stat to junction,</string>
	<string id=8 seek=1933692>then select a magic to

	<string id=9 seek=1933740>However,</string>
	<string id=10 seek=1933752>magic with no status change,

	<string id=11 seek=1933816>Status junction affects

	<string id=14 seek=1933932>The status change probability is

	<string id=15 seek=1933984>In the example, there is a 90% chance

	<string id=16 seek=1934060>100% is the maximum value, but there

	<string id=17 seek=1934160>Junctioning to ST-Def</string>

	<string id=19 seek=1934228>Probability is displayed in %.

	<string id=20 seek=1934296>In the example, the effect of Sleep

	<string id=21 seek=1934360>However, depending on the enemy attack,

	<string id=23 seek=1934520>Some magic, like Esuna, will

	<string id=24 seek=1934592>Try junctioning different
